***ода.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ода.html>о́да</a> (12622)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ᾠδή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ōidḗ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***одалживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживать</a> (29802)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odolžítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odálživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lend <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to allow to be used temporarily</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">мари́на <a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживает</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:незнакомый.html>незнако́мым</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́дям</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Marína nikogdá ne <b>odálživajet</b> dénʹgi neznakómym ljúdjam.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Marina never <b>lends</b> money to strangers.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to borrow <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to receive (something) temporarily</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иногда.html>иногда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзе́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удочка.html>у́дочку</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хоте́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдохнуть.html>отдохну́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:природа.html>приро́де</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On inogdá <b>odálžival</b> u druzéj údočku, kogdá xotél otdoxnútʹ na priróde.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He sometimes <b>borrowed</b> a fishing rod from friends when he wanted to relax outdoors.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The difference between "to lend" and "to borrow" is determined by the context and the usage of prepositions and cases, e.g. "he lends me money" is "<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживает</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a>" ("<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a>" is a dative case) and "he borrows money from me" is "<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживает</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a>" ("<a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a>" is used with the genitive case).</li>
<li>The object of lending/borrowing is normally in the accusative but can also be in the genitive case, especially in the negative clauses.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">both senses</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">одолжа́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odolžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:занимать.html>занима́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zanimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to lend</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взаймы.html>взаймы́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">davátʹ vzajmý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ссужа́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ssužátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>to loan</i>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to borrow</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взаймы.html>взаймы́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bratʹ vzajmý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́л</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжи́ть</a>.

***одаривать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одаривать.html>ода́ривать</a> (25294)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одарить.html>одари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odarítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одаривать.html>ода́ривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odárivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одарить.html>одари́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give presents
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одаривать.html>ода́ривать</a></b> кого́-либо че́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odárivatʹ</b> kovó-libo čém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to present someone with something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to endow <i>(with)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***одарить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одарить.html>одари́ть</a> (13916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дарить.html>дари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">darítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одарить.html>одари́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odarítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">одаря́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одаривать.html>ода́ривать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give presents
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одарить.html>одари́ть</a></b> кого́-либо че́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odarítʹ</b> kovó-libo čém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to present someone with something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to endow <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:природа.html>приро́да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одарить.html>одари́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разнообразный.html>разнообра́зными</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:способность.html>спосо́бностями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">priróda <b>odaríla</b> jevó raznoobráznymi sposóbnostjami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nature has endowed him with a variety of talents</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ри́ть</b>

Зализняка — 4b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:одаривать.html>ода́ривать</a>, одарять.

***одевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одевать.html>одева́ть</a> (12491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одевать.html>одева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dress, to clothe</li>
<li>to provide clothes</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">одевание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odevanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жда</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odéžda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеяние.html>одея́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odejánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

***одежда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жда</a> (1011)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from Old Church Slavonic, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*odeďa</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежа.html>одёжа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odjóža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odéžda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>clothes, clothing, garments</li>
<li>surfacing, top dressing</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежа.html>одёжа</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odjóža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одежка.html>одёжка</a> (19449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежа.html>одёжа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odjóža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежка.html>одёжка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odjóžka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежка.html>одёжки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежка.html>одёжки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежка.html>одёжек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clothes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одежка.html>одёжке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:протягивать.html>протя́гивай</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ножка.html>но́жки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po odjóžke protjágivaj nóžki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cut one's coat according to one's cloth, live within one's means</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одежка.html>одёжке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́ют</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>уму́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:провожать.html>провожа́ют</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po odjóžke vstrečájut, a po umú provožájut</i> ― <span class="e-translation">clothes count for first impressions only</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одергивать.html>одёргивать</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:одернуть.html>одёрнуть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>о-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-дёрг-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ива</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одеревенеть.html>одеревене́ть</a> (21789)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">деревене́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">derevenétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеревенеть.html>одеревене́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oderevenétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">деревене́ть</b>)

<li>to get numb</li>
<li>to lignify, to become wood</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a> (11438)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">deržátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>to win, to gain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верх</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oderžátʹ</b> verx nad kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to prevail over someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oderžátʹ</b> pobédu nad kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to win a victory over someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:дер.html>дер</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жа́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 5c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:одерживать.html>оде́рживать</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-одерж-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***одерживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одерживать.html>оде́рживать</a> (29676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одерживать.html>оде́рживать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odérživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to win, to gain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одерживать.html>оде́рживать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верх</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odérživatʹ</b> verx nad kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to prevail over someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одерживать.html>оде́рживать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odérživatʹ</b> pobédu nad kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to win a victory over someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержи́мый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oderžímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержимость.html>одержи́мость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oderžímostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержимость.html>одержи́мости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержимость.html>одержи́мости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержимость.html>одержи́мостей</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержи́мый</a> (12027)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́мый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержи́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oderžímyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>possessed <i>(by)</i>, obsessed (by)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержи́мый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>стра́хом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oderžímyj</b> stráxom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ridden by fear</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одесский.html>оде́сский</a> (8255)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">оде́сса</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Odéssa, odɛ́ssa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Odessa</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">adjectival suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одесский.html>оде́сский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odésskij, odɛ́sskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Odessa; Odessan</li></ol>

***одеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a> (10739)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*oděti</i>, equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деть.html>деть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">detʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одевать.html>одева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dress, to clothe
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:теплый.html>тепло́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">detéj <b>odéli</b> tepló</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the children had been <b>dressed</b> warmly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to provide clothes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бедняга.html>бедня́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:накормить.html>накорми́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bednjágu nádo nakormítʹ i <b>odétʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the poor fellow needs to be fed and <b>given clothes</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1833</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a>. Пушкин (Alexander Pushkin),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:осень.html>О́сень</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> багре́ц <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:золото.html>зо́лото</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одетый.html>оде́тые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>леса́</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V bagréc i zóloto <b>odétyje</b> lesá</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Woods <b>covered</b> in crimson and gold</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> proscribed</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put on <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">clothing, equipment</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шапка.html>ша́пку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>odél</b> na gólovu šápku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he <b>put on</b> a hat</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Usage of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a> (что-либо)</b> in the sense of <i>to put on (something)</i> is considered non-standard in modern Russian; <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надеть.html>наде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> should be used instead.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">одевание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odevanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеться.html>оде́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odétʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеваться.html>одева́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odevátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жда</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odéžda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеяние.html>одея́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odejánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:деть.html>де́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 15a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:одевать.html>одева́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>о-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-де-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
